    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">MaxNameLen</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">:</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0x0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">MaxClassLen</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; </span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">:</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0x0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">MaxValueNameLen</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; </span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0x8</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">MaxValueDataLen</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; </span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0x66</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">LastWriteTime</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp; </span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0x</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">1d861d2:0xdb7718d1</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">SubKeyCount[Stable</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;
        </span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">]:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0x0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">SubKeyLists[Stable</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;
        </span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">]:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0xffffffff</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">SubKeyCount[Volatile]:</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0x0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">SubKeyLists[Volatile]:</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0xffffffff</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ValueList.Count</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; </span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0x3</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ValueList.List</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp;</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c6">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0xe825a8</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c5 WuvYfpVbPj-c4"></span></p><br>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c8"><span>A very similar effect can be achieved by finding the Registry process, switching to
            its context, and inspecting the memory directly by overlaying it onto the
        </span><span>CM_KEY_NODE</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c5 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp;structure layout:</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c8 WuvYfpVbPj-c10"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c5 WuvYfpVbPj-c4"></span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span></span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">kd&gt;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">!process</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">****</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">NT</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ACTIVE</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">PROCESS</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">DUMP</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">****</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">PROCESS</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ffffe30198ef5040</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; &nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">SessionId:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">none</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">Cid:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0004</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; &nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">Peb:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">00000000</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ParentCid:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0000</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; &nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">DirBase:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">001ae002</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ObjectTable:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ffff88877a285f00</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">HandleCount:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">3302.</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; &nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">Image:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">System</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9 WuvYfpVbPj-c10"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c16 WuvYfpVbPj-c4"></span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">PROCESS</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ffffe30198fe1080</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; &nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">SessionId:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">none</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">Cid:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0040</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; &nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">Peb:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">00000000</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ParentCid:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0004</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; &nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">DirBase:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">1002c002</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ObjectTable:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">ffff88877a277b40</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">HandleCount:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; &nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">0.</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp; &nbsp; </span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0">Image:</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c17">&nbsp;</span><span
            class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">Registry</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9 WuvYfpVbPj-c10"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4"></span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">[...]</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9 WuvYfpVbPj-c10"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4"></span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">kd&gt; .process ffffe30198fe1080</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">Implicit process is now ffffe301`98fe1080</span>
    </p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">WARNING: .cache forcedecodeuser is not
            enabled<br></span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">kd&gt; dt _CM_KEY_NODE 1e6ed0334b4</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">nt!_CM_KEY_NODE</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x000 Signature &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp;: 0x6b6e</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x002 Flags &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;: 0x20</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x004 LastWriteTime &nbsp; &nbsp;:
            _LARGE_INTEGER 0x01d861d2`db7718d1</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x00c AccessBits &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; : 0x3 &#39;&#39;</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x00d LayerSemantics &nbsp; :
            0y00</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x00d Spare1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp; : 0y00000 (0)</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x00d InheritClass &nbsp; &nbsp; :
            0y0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x00e Spare2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp; : 0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x010 Parent &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp; : 0x20</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x014 SubKeyCounts &nbsp; &nbsp; :
            [2] 0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x01c SubKeyLists &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp;: [2] 0xffffffff</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x024 ValueList &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp;: _CHILD_LIST</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x01c ChildHiveReference :
            _CM_KEY_REFERENCE</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x02c Security &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; : 0x98f300</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x030 Class &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;: 0xffffffff</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x034 MaxNameLen &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; : 0y0000000000000000 (0)</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x034 UserFlags &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp;: 0y0000</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x034 VirtControlFlags :
            0y0000</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x034 Debug &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;: 0y00000000 (0)</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x038 MaxClassLen &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp;: 0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x03c MaxValueNameLen &nbsp;:
            8</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x040 MaxValueDataLen &nbsp;:
            0x66</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x044 WorkVar &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp;: 0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x048 NameLength &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; : 0x16</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x04a ClassLength &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp;: 0</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c9"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c0 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp; &nbsp;+0x04c Name &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
            &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; : [1] &nbsp;&quot;&#25924;&quot;</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c8"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c5 WuvYfpVbPj-c4"></span></p><br>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c8"><span>In the listing above, we can see the full extent of information stored in the hive
            for each key. The name in the last line is incorrectly displayed as &#25924;, because formally the type of
        </span><span>CM_KEY_NODE.Name</span><span>&nbsp;is </span><span>wchar_t[1]</span><span>, but since the name
            consists of ASCII-only characters, it is compressed down so that each
        </span><span>wchar_t</span><span>&nbsp;element stores two characters of the name (as indicated by the flag 0x20
            translated by WinDbg as </span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c2">CompressedName</span><span>). So &#25924; is in
            fact the two first letter of the name, &quot;De&quot;, represented as a UTF-16 code point.</span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c8 WuvYfpVbPj-c10"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c5 WuvYfpVbPj-c4"></span></p>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c8"><span>This is only a glimpse of what is possible with WinDbg and the
        </span><span>!reg</span><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c5 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">&nbsp;extension. I highly encourage you to
            experiment with other options if you&#39;re curious about the mechanics of the registry and want to explore
            further.</span></p>
    <h2 class="WuvYfpVbPj-c15 WuvYfpVbPj-c14" id="h.w0749erpaz1u"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c1">Conclusion</span></h2>
    <p class="WuvYfpVbPj-c8"><span class="WuvYfpVbPj-c5 WuvYfpVbPj-c4">In this post, I have aimed to share my
            methodology for gathering information and learning about new vulnerability research targets. I hope that you
            find some of it useful, either as a generalized approach that applies to other software, or as a
            comprehensive knowledge base for the registry itself. Also, if you think I&#39;ve missed any resources,
            I&#39;ll be more than happy to learn about them. See you in the next post!</span></p>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<a class='post-count-link' href='https://googleprojectzero.blogspot.com/2014/07/'>
July
</a>
<span class='post-count' dir='ltr'>(3)</span>

<script type='text/javascript'>
//<![CDATA[
(function(){
  let archive_list = document.getElementById('ArchiveList');
  if (archive_list == null) return;
  let cur_year = archive_list.querySelector('.post-count-link').innerText.trim() - 0;
  let last_year = 2014;
  let elements = [];
  const MONTHS = ',Jan,Feb,Mar,Apr,May,Jun,Jul,Aug,Sep,Oct,Nov,Dec'.split(',');

  let parent = document.getElementById('ArchiveList');
  while (parent.childNodes.length) parent.removeChild(parent.childNodes[0]);

  function fetch_next_year() {
    let url = 'https://googleprojectzero.blogspot.com/?action=getTitles&widgetId=BlogArchive1&widgetType=BlogArchive&responseType=js&path=https%3A%2F%2Fgoogleprojectzero.blogspot.com%2F'+cur_year;
    fetch(url).then(resp => {
      if (!resp.ok) {
        console.log('http error');
        return;
      }
      resp.text().then(text => {
        let scope = {
          _WidgetManager: {
            _HandleControllerResult: (name, method, results) => {
              elements.push(document.createElement('hr'));
              let year_header = document.createElement('div');
              year_header.appendChild(document.createTextNode(cur_year));
              year_header.style.fontSize = 'large';
              elements.push(year_header);

              let list = document.createElement('ul');
              elements.push(list);

              for (let obj of results.posts) {
                let link_parts = obj.url.split('/');
                let year = link_parts[3];
                let month = link_parts[4];

                let el = document.createElement(/*'div'*/'li');
                el.style.listStyleType = 'square';
                el.style.listStylePosition = 'inside';
                let link = document.createElement('a');
                el.appendChild(link);
                link.appendChild(document.createTextNode(obj.title));
                link.href = obj.url;
                let date_trailer = document.createElement('span');
                el.appendChild(date_trailer);
                //date_trailer.appendChild(document.createTextNode(' ('+year+'-'+month+')'));
                date_trailer.appendChild(document.createTextNode(' ('+MONTHS[parseInt(month, 10)]+')'));
                //date_trailer.style.textAlign = 'right';
                //elements.push(el);
                list.appendChild(el);
              }
            }
          }
        };
        with (scope) { eval(text); }
        if (cur_year == last_year) {
          finish();
        } else {
          cur_year--;
          fetch_next_year();
        }
      });
    });
  }
  fetch_next_year();
  function finish() {
    for (let obj of elements) {
      parent.appendChild(obj);
    }
    console.log(elements);
  }
})();
//]]>
</script>
